INPUT: === user_task_description ===

# Requirements Document for 'TravelPlanner' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'TravelPlanner' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse destinations, plan itineraries, search accommodations, book flights, view travel packages, and manage trip details. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'TravelPlanner' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'TravelPlanner' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Planner Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured destinations, upcoming trips, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-destinations** - Type: Div - Display of featured travel destinations.
  - **ID: upcoming-trips** - Type: Div - Display of upcoming planned trips.
  - **ID: browse-destinations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to destinations page.
  - **ID: plan-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to itinerary planning page.

### 2. Destinations Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Destinations
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available travel destinations with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: destinations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the destinations page.
  - **ID: search-destination** - Type: Input - Field to search destinations by name or country.
  - **ID: region-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by region (Asia, Europe, Americas, Africa, Oceania).
  - **ID: destinations-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying destination cards with image, name, and country.
  - **ID: view-destination-button-{dest_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view destination details (each destination card has this).

### 3. Destination Details Page
- **Page Title**: Destination Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific destination.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: destination-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the destination details page.
  - **ID: destination-name** - Type: H1 - Display destination name.
  - **ID: destination-country** - Type: Div - Display destination country.
  - **ID: destination-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description of the destination.
  - **ID: add-to-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to add destination to trip.
  - **ID: destination-attractions** - Type: Div - Section displaying main attractions and activities.

### 4. Itinerary Planning Page
- **Page Title**: Plan Your Itinerary
- **Overview**: A page for users to create and manage travel itineraries with activities and schedules.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: itinerary-page** - Type: Div - Container for the itinerary page.
  - **ID: itinerary-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to enter itinerary name.
  - **ID: start-date-input** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select trip start date.
  - **ID: end-date-input** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select trip end date.
  - **ID: add-activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to add activity to itinerary.
  - **ID: itinerary-list** - Type: Div - Display list of created itineraries with edit/delete options.

### 5. Accommodations Page
- **Page Title**: Search Accommodations
- **Overview**: A page for searching and browsing hotel options with filters and pricing.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: accommodations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the accommodations page.
  - **ID: destination-input** - Type: Input - Field to enter destination city for hotels.
  - **ID: check-in-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select check-in date.
  - **ID: check-out-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select check-out date.
  - **ID: price-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter hotels by price range (Budget, Mid-range, Luxury).
  - **ID: hotels-list** - Type: Div - List of available hotels with name, rating, price, and amenities.

### 6. Transportation Page
- **Page Title**: Book Flights
- **Overview**: A page for searching and booking flights with departure and arrival options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: transportation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the transportation page.
  - **ID: departure-city** - Type: Input - Field to enter departure city.
  - **ID: arrival-city** - Type: Input - Field to enter arrival city.
  - **ID: departure-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select departure date.
  - **ID: flight-class-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by flight class (Economy, Business, First Class).
  - **ID: available-flights** - Type: Div - List of available flights with airlines, times, and prices.

### 7. Travel Packages Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Packages
- **Overview**: A page displaying pre-designed travel packages with complete trip information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: packages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the packages page.
  - **ID: packages-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying travel package cards with destination, duration, and price.
  - **ID: duration-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter packages by duration (3-5 days, 7-10 days, 14+ days).
  - **ID: view-package-details-button-{pkg_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view package details (each package has this).
  - **ID: book-package-button-{pkg_id}** - Type: Button - Button to book selected package (each package has this).

### 8. Trip Management Page
- **Page Title**: My Trips
- **Overview**: A page displaying all created trips with options to view, edit, or delete them.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: trips-page** - Type: Div - Container for the trips page.
  - **ID: trips-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all trips with destination, dates, and status.
  - **ID: view-trip-details-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view trip details (each trip has this).
  - **ID: edit-trip-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to edit trip (each trip has this).
  - **ID: delete-trip-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete trip (each trip has this).

### 9. Booking Confirmation Page
- **Page Title**: Booking Confirmation
- **Overview**: A page displaying booking confirmation details with reservation information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: confirmation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the confirmation page.
  - **ID: confirmation-number** - Type: Div - Display confirmation/booking number.
  - **ID: booking-details** - Type: Div - Display detailed booking information (dates, amounts, locations).
  - **ID: download-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to download trip itinerary as PDF.
  - **ID: share-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to share trip details.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Travel Recommendations Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Recommendations
- **Overview**: A page displaying personalized travel recommendations and trending destinations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: recommendations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the recommendations page.
  - **ID: trending-destinations** - Type: Div - Display trending destinations ranked by popularity.
  - **ID: recommendation-season-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by travel season (Spring, Summer, Fall, Winter).
  - **ID: budget-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by budget range (Low, Medium, High).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'TravelPlanner' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Destinations Data
- **File Name**: `destinations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  dest_id|name|country|region|description|attractions|climate
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Paris|France|Europe|City of lights and romance with world-class museums|Eiffel Tower, Louvre Museum, Notre-Dame|Temperate
  2|Tokyo|Japan|Asia|Modern metropolis blending tradition and innovation|Senso-ji Temple, Shibuya Crossing, Meiji Shrine|Temperate
  3|Rio de Janeiro|Brazil|Americas|Vibrant beach city with iconic landmarks|Christ the Redeemer, Copacabana Beach, Sugarloaf Mountain|Tropical
  ```

### 2. Itineraries Data
- **File Name**: `itineraries.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  itinerary_id|itinerary_name|destination|start_date|end_date|activities|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Paris Spring Break|Paris|2025-03-20|2025-03-27|Museum tours, River cruise, Cafe hopping|Planned
  2|Tokyo Adventure|Tokyo|2025-05-01|2025-05-14|Temple visits, Anime district tour, Cooking class|In Progress
  3|Rio Beach Trip|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-15|2025-07-22|Beach days, Hiking, Night clubs|Planned
  ```

### 3. Hotels Data
- **File Name**: `hotels.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  hotel_id|name|city|rating|price_per_night|amenities|category
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Ritz Paris|Paris|5.0|450.00|WiFi, Spa, Restaurant, Pool|Luxury
  2|Hotel Shibuya|Tokyo|4.5|120.00|WiFi, Cafe, Business Center|Mid-range
  3|Copacabana Beach Hotel|Rio de Janeiro|4.0|95.00|Beach access, Restaurant, WiFi|Mid-range
  ```

### 4. Flights Data
- **File Name**: `flights.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  flight_id|airline|departure_city|arrival_city|departure_time|arrival_time|price|class_type|duration
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Air France|New York|Paris|10:00|22:30|850.00|Economy|7 hours 30 minutes
  2|JAL|Los Angeles|Tokyo|14:30|15:20 next day|920.00|Business|11 hours 50 minutes
  3|Latam|Miami|Rio de Janeiro|18:00|23:45|380.00|Economy|5 hours 45 minutes
  ```

### 5. Travel Packages Data
- **File Name**: `packages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  package_id|package_name|destination|duration_days|price|included_items|difficulty_level
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Paris Classic Tour|Paris|5|1500.00|Hotel, Flights, Guided tours, Meals|Easy
  2|Tokyo Experience|Tokyo|10|2200.00|Hotel, Flights, Activities, Cultural events|Moderate
  3|Rio Adventure|Rio de Janeiro|7|1800.00|Hotel, Flights, Beach activities, Mountain hiking|Moderate
  ```

### 6. Trips Data
- **File Name**: `trips.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  trip_id|trip_name|destination|start_date|end_date|total_budget|status|created_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Summer Vacation 2025|Paris|2025-06-01|2025-06-15|3000.00|Booked|2025-01-10
  2|Winter Holiday|Tokyo|2025-12-15|2025-12-30|4500.00|Planned|2025-01-11
  3|Beach Getaway|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-01|2025-07-08|2000.00|Pending|2025-01-12
  ```

### 7. Bookings Data
- **File Name**: `bookings.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  booking_id|trip_id|booking_type|booking_date|amount|confirmation_number|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Hotel|2025-01-10|750.00|CONF001|Confirmed
  2|2|Flight|2025-01-11|1840.00|CONF002|Confirmed
  3|3|Package|2025-01-12|1800.00|CONF003|Pending
  ```

## 1. HTML Templates Specification

## 2. File Data Schemas

### 2.1 destinations.txt

- **Example:**
  ```
  1|Paris|France|Europe|City of romance and museums|Eiffel Tower, Louvre|Temperate
  2|Rio de Janeiro|Brazil|Americas|Vibrant city with famous landmarks|Christ the Redeemer, Copacabana|Tropical
  ```

### 2.2 itineraries.txt
- **Format:** itinerary_id|itinerary_name|destination|start_date|end_date|activities|status
- **Example:**
  ```
  1|Spring Adventure|Tokyo|2025-05-01|2025-05-14|Temple visits, Anime tours|In Progress
  2|Beach Relaxation|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-15|2025-07-22|Beach hiking, Night clubs|Planned
  ```

### 2.3 hotels.txt
- **Format:** hotel_id|name|location|rating|price|amenities|category
- **Example:**
  ```
  1|Ritz|Paris|4.5|250.00|Spa, Business Center|Luxury
  2|Copacabana Beach Hotel|Rio de Janeiro|4.0|95.00|Beach access, WiFi|Mid-range
  ```

### 2.4 flights.txt
- **Format:** flight_id|airline|departure_city|arrival_city|departure_time|arrival_time|price|class_type|duration
- **Example:**
  ```
  1|Air France|Paris|New York|08:00|11:00|450.00|Economy|7h
  2|Latam|Miami|Rio de Janeiro|18:00|23:45|380.00|Economy|5h 45m
  ```

### 2.5 packages.txt
- **Format:** package_id|package_name|destination|duration_days|price|included_items|difficulty_level
- **Example:**
  ```
  1|Paris Classic Tour|Paris|5|1500.00|Hotel, Tours, Meals|Easy
  2|Tokyo Adventure|Tokyo|7|2000.00|Activities, Cultural events|Moderate
  ```

### 2.6 trips.txt
- **Format:** trip_id|trip_name|destination|start_date|end_date|total_budget|status|created_date
- **Example:**
  ```
  1|Vacation 2025|Paris|2025-06-01|2025-06-15|3000.00|Booked|2025-01-10
  2|Winter Holiday|Tokyo|2025-12-15|2025-12-30|4500.00|Planned|2025-01-11
  ```

### 2.7 bookings.txt
- **Format:** booking_id|trip_id|booking_type|booking_date|amount|confirmation_number|status
- **Example:**
  ```
  1|1|Hotel|2025-01-10|750.00|CONF001|Confirmed
  2|2|Flight|2025-01-11|1840.00|CONF002|Confirmed
  ```

This design spec fully details the HTML template elements with IDs, filenames, page titles, and explicit data file schemas suited for backend/frontend development of TravelPlanner.

  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'TravelPlanner' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'TravelPlanner' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse destinations, plan itineraries, search accommodations, book flights, view travel packages, and manage trip details. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'TravelPlanner' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'TravelPlanner' web application will consist of the following ten pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Travel Planner Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured destinations, upcoming trips, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-destinations** - Type: Div - Display of featured travel destinations.   - **ID: upcoming-trips** - Type: Div - Display of upcoming planned trips.   - **ID: browse-destinations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to destinations page.   - **ID: plan-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to itinerary planning page.  ### 2. Destinations Page - **Page Title**: Travel Destinations - **Overview**: A page displaying all available travel destinations with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: destinations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the destinations page.   - **ID: search-destination** - Type: Input - Field to search destinations by name or country.   - **ID: region-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by region (Asia, Europe, Americas, Africa, Oceania).   - **ID: destinations-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying destination cards with image, name, and country.   - **ID: view-destination-button-{dest_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view destination details (each destination card has this).  ### 3. Destination Details Page - **Page Title**: Destination Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific destination. - **Elements**:   - **ID: destination-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the destination details page.   - **ID: destination-name** - Type: H1 - Display destination name.   - **ID: destination-country** - Type: Div - Display destination country.   - **ID: destination-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description of the destination.   - **ID: add-to-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to add destination to trip.   - **ID: destination-attractions** - Type: Div - Section displaying main attractions and activities.  ### 4. Itinerary Planning Page - **Page Title**: Plan Your Itinerary - **Overview**: A page for users to create and manage travel itineraries with activities and schedules. - **Elements**:   - **ID: itinerary-page** - Type: Div - Container for the itinerary page.   - **ID: itinerary-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to enter itinerary name.   - **ID: start-date-input** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select trip start date.   - **ID: end-date-input** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select trip end date.   - **ID: add-activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to add activity to itinerary.   - **ID: itinerary-list** - Type: Div - Display list of created itineraries with edit/delete options.  ### 5. Accommodations Page - **Page Title**: Search Accommodations - **Overview**: A page for searching and browsing hotel options with filters and pricing. - **Elements**:   - **ID: accommodations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the accommodations page.   - **ID: destination-input** - Type: Input - Field to enter destination city for hotels.   - **ID: check-in-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select check-in date.   - **ID: check-out-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select check-out date.   - **ID: price-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter hotels by price range (Budget, Mid-range, Luxury).   - **ID: hotels-list** - Type: Div - List of available hotels with name, rating, price, and amenities.  ### 6. Transportation Page - **Page Title**: Book Flights - **Overview**: A page for searching and booking flights with departure and arrival options. - **Elements**:   - **ID: transportation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the transportation page.   - **ID: departure-city** - Type: Input - Field to enter departure city.   - **ID: arrival-city** - Type: Input - Field to enter arrival city.   - **ID: departure-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select departure date.   - **ID: flight-class-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by flight class (Economy, Business, First Class).   - **ID: available-flights** - Type: Div - List of available flights with airlines, times, and prices.  ### 7. Travel Packages Page - **Page Title**: Travel Packages - **Overview**: A page displaying pre-designed travel packages with complete trip information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: packages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the packages page.   - **ID: packages-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying travel package cards with destination, duration, and price.   - **ID: duration-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter packages by duration (3-5 days, 7-10 days, 14+ days).   - **ID: view-package-details-button-{pkg_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view package details (each package has this).   - **ID: book-package-button-{pkg_id}** - Type: Button - Button to book selected package (each package has this).  ### 8. Trip Management Page - **Page Title**: My Trips - **Overview**: A page displaying all created trips with options to view, edit, or delete them. - **Elements**:   - **ID: trips-page** - Type: Div - Container for the trips page.   - **ID: trips-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all trips with destination, dates, and status.   - **ID: view-trip-details-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view trip details (each trip has this).   - **ID: edit-trip-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to edit trip (each trip has this).   - **ID: delete-trip-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete trip (each trip has this).  ### 9. Booking Confirmation Page - **Page Title**: Booking Confirmation - **Overview**: A page displaying booking confirmation details with reservation information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: confirmation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the confirmation page.   - **ID: confirmation-number** - Type: Div - Display confirmation/booking number.   - **ID: booking-details** - Type: Div - Display detailed booking information (dates, amounts, locations).   - **ID: download-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to download trip itinerary as PDF.   - **ID: share-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to share trip details.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 10. Travel Recommendations Page - **Page Title**: Travel Recommendations - **Overview**: A page displaying personalized travel recommendations and trending destinations. - **Elements**:   - **ID: recommendations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the recommendations page.   - **ID: trending-destinations** - Type: Div - Display trending destinations ranked by popularity.   - **ID: recommendation-season-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by travel season (Spring, Summer, Fall, Winter).   - **ID: budget-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by budget range (Low, Medium, High).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'TravelPlanner' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Destinations Data - **File Name**: `destinations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   dest_id|name|country|region|description|attractions|climate   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Paris|France|Europe|City of lights and romance with world-class museums|Eiffel Tower, Louvre Museum, Notre-Dame|Temperate   2|Tokyo|Japan|Asia|Modern metropolis blending tradition and innovation|Senso-ji Temple, Shibuya Crossing, Meiji Shrine|Temperate   3|Rio de Janeiro|Brazil|Americas|Vibrant beach city with iconic landmarks|Christ the Redeemer, Copacabana Beach, Sugarloaf Mountain|Tropical   ```  ### 2. Itineraries Data - **File Name**: `itineraries.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   itinerary_id|itinerary_name|destination|start_date|end_date|activities|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Paris Spring Break|Paris|2025-03-20|2025-03-27|Museum tours, River cruise, Cafe hopping|Planned   2|Tokyo Adventure|Tokyo|2025-05-01|2025-05-14|Temple visits, Anime district tour, Cooking class|In Progress   3|Rio Beach Trip|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-15|2025-07-22|Beach days, Hiking, Night clubs|Planned   ```  ### 3. Hotels Data - **File Name**: `hotels.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   hotel_id|name|city|rating|price_per_night|amenities|category   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Ritz Paris|Paris|5.0|450.00|WiFi, Spa, Restaurant, Pool|Luxury   2|Hotel Shibuya|Tokyo|4.5|120.00|WiFi, Cafe, Business Center|Mid-range   3|Copacabana Beach Hotel|Rio de Janeiro|4.0|95.00|Beach access, Restaurant, WiFi|Mid-range   ```  ### 4. Flights Data - **File Name**: `flights.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   flight_id|airline|departure_city|arrival_city|departure_time|arrival_time|price|class_type|duration   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Air France|New York|Paris|10:00|22:30|850.00|Economy|7 hours 30 minutes   2|JAL|Los Angeles|Tokyo|14:30|15:20 next day|920.00|Business|11 hours 50 minutes   3|Latam|Miami|Rio de Janeiro|18:00|23:45|380.00|Economy|5 hours 45 minutes   ```  ### 5. Travel Packages Data - **File Name**: `packages.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   package_id|package_name|destination|duration_days|price|included_items|difficulty_level   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Paris Classic Tour|Paris|5|1500.00|Hotel, Flights, Guided tours, Meals|Easy   2|Tokyo Experience|Tokyo|10|2200.00|Hotel, Flights, Activities, Cultural events|Moderate   3|Rio Adventure|Rio de Janeiro|7|1800.00|Hotel, Flights, Beach activities, Mountain hiking|Moderate   ```  ### 6. Trips Data - **File Name**: `trips.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   trip_id|trip_name|destination|start_date|end_date|total_budget|status|created_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Summer Vacation 2025|Paris|2025-06-01|2025-06-15|3000.00|Booked|2025-01-10   2|Winter Holiday|Tokyo|2025-12-15|2025-12-30|4500.00|Planned|2025-01-11   3|Beach Getaway|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-01|2025-07-08|2000.00|Pending|2025-01-12   ```  ### 7. Bookings Data - **File Name**: `bookings.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   booking_id|trip_id|booking_type|booking_date|amount|confirmation_number|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Hotel|2025-01-10|750.00|CONF001|Confirmed   2|2|Flight|2025-01-11|1840.00|CONF002|Confirmed   3|3|Package|2025-01-12|1800.00|CONF003|Pending   ```
  [design_spec.md] # TravelPlanner Design Specification  ## 1. HTML Templates Specification  ### 1.1 Dashboard Page - **Filename:** dashboard.html - **Page Title:** Dashboard - **Description:** Main page with featured destinations and quick navigation. - **Elements:**   - Div container with ID `dashboard-container` - wraps the whole page.   - Div with ID `featured-destinations` - displays highlighted destinations.   - Div with ID `recent-trips` - displays recent trips summary.   - Button with ID `browse-destinations-button` - navigates to `/destinations`.   - Button with ID `plan-itinerary-button` - navigates to `/itinerary`.  ### 1.2 Destinations Page - **Filename:** destinations.html - **Page Title:** Destinations - **Description:** Lists destinations with search and filtering. - **Elements:**   - Div with ID `destinations-container` - container for all destinations.   - Input search field with ID `search-destination` - text input to search by name.   - Dropdown with ID `region-filter` - filter for regions (Asia, Europe, Africa, Americas, Oceania).   - Buttons with ID pattern `view-destination-button-{{ dest.dest_id }}` - button to view details for each destination.  ### 1.3 Destination Detail Page - **Filename:** destination_detail.html - **Page Title:** Destination Detail - **Description:** Detailed information of selected destination. - **Elements:**   - Heading (H1) with ID `destination-name` - destination name.   - Div with ID `destination-country` - displays country.   - Div with ID `destination-description` - detailed description.   - Div with ID `destination-attractions` - attractions list.   - Button with ID `add-to-trip-button` - adds destination to trip.  ### 1.4 Itinerary Page - **Filename:** itinerary.html - **Page Title:** Your Itinerary - **Description:** Create and edit itineraries. - **Elements:**   - Input with ID `itinerary-name-input` - itinerary name input.   - Input with ID `start-date-input` (type date) - itinerary start date.   - Input with ID `end-date-input` (type date) - itinerary end date.   - Button with ID `add-activity-button` - add activity to itinerary.   - Div with ID `activities-container` - lists added activities.  ### 1.5 Accommodations Page - **Filename:** accommodations.html - **Page Title:** Accommodations - **Description:** Search and filter available hotels. - **Elements:**   - Div with ID `accommodations-container` - container for hotels.   - Input with ID `check-in-date` (date) - check-in date.   - Input with ID `check-out-date` (date) - check-out date.   - Dropdown with ID `price-filter` - filter by budget (Budget, Mid-range, Luxury).  ### 1.6 Transportation Page - **Filename:** transportation.html - **Page Title:** Flights - **Description:** Search flights by departure/arrival and booking options. - **Elements:**   - Input with ID `departure-city-input` - departure city.   - Input with ID `arrival-city-input` - arrival city.   - Input with ID `departure-date` (date) - departure date.   - Dropdown with ID `flight-class-filter` - flight class (Economy, Business, First).  ### 1.7 Packages Page - **Filename:** packages.html - **Page Title:** Travel Packages - **Description:** Lists pre-designed travel packages with filters. - **Elements:**   - Div with ID `packages-grid` - grid container for packages.   - Dropdown with ID `duration-filter` - filter packages by duration (3-5 days, 7-10 days).   - Buttons with ID pattern `view-package-button-{{ package.package_id }}` - button to view package details.  ### 1.8 Trips Page - **Filename:** trips.html - **Page Title:** Trips - **Description:** Manage and view all trips. - **Elements:**   - Div with ID `trips-container` - container for trips.   - Table with ID `trips-table` - show trip summaries.   - Buttons with ID pattern `view-trip-details-button-{{ trip.trip_id }}`, `edit-trip-button-{{ trip.trip_id }}`, `delete-trip-button-{{ trip.trip_id }}` - trip actions.  ### 1.9 Booking Confirmation Page - **Filename:** booking_confirmation.html - **Page Title:** Booking Confirmation - **Description:** Displays booking confirmation details. - **Elements:**   - Div with ID `confirmation-page` - confirmation container.   - Div with ID `confirmation-number` - booking confirmation number.   - Div with ID `booking-details` - detailed booking info.   - Button with ID `download-itinerary-button` - download itinerary PDF.   - Button with ID `back-to-dashboard` - navigate to dashboard.  ### 1.10 Recommendations Page - **Filename:** recommendations.html - **Page Title:** Recommendations - **Description:** Personalized travel recommendations with filters. - **Elements:**   - Div with ID `recommendations-container` - container for recommendations.   - Dropdown with ID `recommendation-season-filter` - seasonal filter.   - Dropdown with ID `budget-filter` - budget filter (Low, Medium, High).   - Button with ID `apply-filter-button` - apply selected filters.   - Button with ID `back-to-dashboard` - navigate to dashboard.  ## 2. File Data Schemas  ### 2.1 destinations.txt - **Format:** dest_id|name|country|region|description|attractions|climate - **Example:**   ```   1|Paris|France|Europe|City of romance and museums|Eiffel Tower, Louvre|Temperate   2|Rio de Janeiro|Brazil|Americas|Vibrant city with famous landmarks|Christ the Redeemer, Copacabana|Tropical   ```  ### 2.2 itineraries.txt - # Requirements Document for 'TravelPlanner' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'TravelPlanner' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse destinations, plan itineraries, search accommodations, book flights, view travel packages, and manage trip details. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'TravelPlanner' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'TravelPlanner' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Planner Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured destinations, upcoming trips, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-destinations** - Type: Div - Display of featured travel destinations.
  - **ID: upcoming-trips** - Type: Div - Display of upcoming planned trips.
  - **ID: browse-destinations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to destinations page.
  - **ID: plan-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to itinerary planning page.

### 2. Destinations Page

- **Overview**: A page displaying all available travel destinations with search and filter capabilities.

  - **ID: search-destination** - Type: Input - Field to search destinations by name or country.
  - **ID: region-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by region (Asia, Europe, Americas, Africa, Oceania).
  - **ID: destinations-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying destination cards with image, name, and country.
  - **ID: view-destination-button-{dest_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view destination details (each destination card has this).

### 3. Destination Details Page
- **Page Title**: Destination Details

### 6. Transportation Page

  - **ID: available-flights** - Type: Div - List of available flights with airlines, times, and prices.

### 7. Travel Packages Page

  - **ID: download-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to download trip itinerary as PDF.
  - **ID: share-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to share trip details.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Travel Recommendations Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Recommendations
- **Overview**: A page displaying personalized travel recommendations and trending destinations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: recommendations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the recommendations page.
  - **ID: trending-destinations** - Type: Div - Display trending destinations ranked by popularity.
  - **ID: recommendation-season-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by travel season (Spring, Summer, Fall, Winter).
  - **ID: budget-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by budget range (Low, Medium, High).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'TravelPlanner' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Destinations Data
- **File Name**: `destinations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  dest_id|name|country|region|description|attractions|climate
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Paris|France|Europe|City of lights and romance with world-class museums|Eiffel Tower, Louvre Museum, Notre-Dame|Temperate
  2|Tokyo|Japan|Asia|Modern metropolis blending tradition and innovation|Senso-ji Temple, Shibuya Crossing, Meiji Shrine|Temperate
  3|Rio de Janeiro|Brazil|Americas|Vibrant beach city with iconic landmarks|Christ the Redeemer, Copacabana Beach, Sugarloaf Mountain|Tropical
  ```

### 2. Itineraries Data
- **File Name**: `itineraries.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  itinerary_id|itinerary_name|destination|start_date|end_date|activities|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Paris Spring Break|Paris|2025-03-20|2025-03-27|Museum tours, River cruise, Cafe hopping|Planned
  2|Tokyo Adventure|Tokyo|2025-05-01|2025-05-14|Temple visits, Anime district tour, Cooking class|In Progress
  3|Rio Beach Trip|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-15|2025-07-22|Beach days, Hiking, Night clubs|Planned
  ```

### 3. Hotels Data
- **File Name**: `hotels.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  hotel_id|name|city|rating|price_per_night|amenities|category
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Ritz Paris|Paris|5.0|450.00|WiFi, Spa, Restaurant, Pool|Luxury
  2|Hotel Shibuya|Tokyo|4.5|120.00|WiFi, Cafe, Business Center|Mid-range
  3|Copacabana Beach Hotel|Rio de Janeiro|4.0|95.00|Beach access, Restaurant, WiFi|Mid-range
  ```

### 4. Flights Data
- **File Name**: `flights.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  flight_id|airline|departure_city|arrival_city|departure_time|arrival_time|price|class_type|duration
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Air France|New York|Paris|10:00|22:30|850.00|Economy|7 hours 30 minutes
  2|JAL|Los Angeles|Tokyo|14:30|15:20 next day|920.00|Business|11 hours 50 minutes
  3|Latam|Miami|Rio de Janeiro|18:00|23:45|380.00|Economy|5 hours 45 minutes
  ```

### 5. Travel Packages Data
- **File Name**: `packages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  package_id|package_name|destination|duration_days|price|included_items|difficulty_level
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Paris Classic Tour|Paris|5|1500.00|Hotel, Flights, Guided tours, Meals|Easy
  2|Tokyo Experience|Tokyo|10|2200.00|Hotel, Flights, Activities, Cultural events|Moderate
  3|Rio Adventure|Rio de Janeiro|7|1800.00|Hotel, Flights, Beach activities, Mountain hiking|Moderate
  ```

### 6. Trips Data
- **File Name**: `trips.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  trip_id|trip_name|destination|start_date|end_date|total_budget|status|created_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Summer Vacation 2025|Paris|2025-06-01|2025-06-15|3000.00|Booked|2025-01-10
  2|Winter Holiday|Tokyo|2025-12-15|2025-12-30|4500.00|Planned|2025-01-11
  3|Beach Getaway|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-01|2025-07-08|2000.00|Pending|2025-01-12
  ```

### 7. Bookings Data
- **File Name**: `bookings.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  booking_id|trip_id|booking_type|booking_date|amount|confirmation_number|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Hotel|2025-01-10|750.00|CONF001|Confirmed
  2|2|Flight|2025-01-11|1840.00|CONF002|Confirmed
  3|3|Package|2025-01-12|1800.00|CONF003|Pending
  ```

# TravelPlanner Design Specification

## 1. HTML Templates Specification

### 1.1 Dashboard Page
- **Filename:** dashboard.html
- **Page Title:** Dashboard
- **Description:** Main page with featured destinations and quick navigation.
- **Elements:**
  - Div container with ID `dashboard-container` - wraps the whole page.
  - Div with ID `featured-destinations` - displays highlighted destinations.
  - Div with ID `recent-trips` - displays recent trips summary.
  - Button with ID `browse-destinations-button` - navigates to `/destinations`.
  - Button with ID `plan-itinerary-button` - navigates to `/itinerary`.

- **Filename:** destinations.html
- **Page Title:** Destinations
- **Description:** Lists destinations with search and filtering.
- **Elements:**
  - Div with ID `destinations-container` - container for all destinations.
  - Input search field with ID `search-destination` - text input to search by name.
  - Dropdown with ID `region-filter` - filter for regions (Asia, Europe, Africa, Americas, Oceania).
  - Buttons with ID pattern `view-destination-button-{{ dest.dest_id }}` - button to view details for each destination.

### 1.3 Destination Detail Page
- **Filename:** destination_detail.html
- **Page Title:** Destination Detail
- **Description:** Detailed information of selected destination.
- **Elements:**
  - Heading (H1) with ID `destination-name` - destination name.
  - Div with ID `destination-country` - displays country.
  - Div with ID `destination-description` - detailed description.
  - Div with ID `destination-attractions` - attractions list.

- **Page Title:** Your Itinerary
- **Description:** Create and edit itineraries.

# Requirements Document for 'TravelPlanner' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'TravelPlanner' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse destinations, plan itineraries, search accommodations, book flights, view travel packages, and manage trip details. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'TravelPlanner' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'TravelPlanner' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Planner Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured destinations, upcoming trips, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-destinations** - Type: Div - Display of featured travel destinations.
  - **ID: upcoming-trips** - Type: Div - Display of upcoming planned trips.
  - **ID: browse-destinations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to destinations page.
  - **ID: plan-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to itinerary planning page.

### 2. Destinations Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Destinations
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available travel destinations with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: destinations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the destinations page.
  - **ID: search-destination** - Type: Input - Field to search destinations by name or country.
  - **ID: region-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by region (Asia, Europe, Americas, Africa, Oceania).
  - **ID: destinations-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying destination cards with image, name, and country.
  - **ID: view-destination-button-{dest_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view destination details (each destination card has this).

### 3. Destination Details Page
- **Page Title**: Destination Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific destination.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: destination-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the destination details page.
  - **ID: destination-name** - Type: H1 - Display destination name.
  - **ID: destination-country** - Type: Div - Display destination country.
  - **ID: destination-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description of the destination.
  - **ID: add-to-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to add destination to trip.
  - **ID: destination-attractions** - Type: Div - Section displaying main attractions and activities.

### 4. Itinerary Planning Page
- **Page Title**: Plan Your Itinerary
- **Overview**: A page for users to create and manage travel itineraries with activities and schedules.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: itinerary-page** - Type: Div - Container for the itinerary page.
  - **ID: itinerary-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to enter itinerary name.
  - **ID: start-date-input** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select trip start date.
  - **ID: end-date-input** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select trip end date.
  - **ID: add-activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to add activity to itinerary.
  - **ID: itinerary-list** - Type: Div - Display list of created itineraries with edit/delete options.

### 5. Accommodations Page
- **Page Title**: Search Accommodations
- **Overview**: A page for searching and browsing hotel options with filters and pricing.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: accommodations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the accommodations page.
  - **ID: destination-input** - Type: Input - Field to enter destination city for hotels.
  - **ID: check-in-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select check-in date.
  - **ID: check-out-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select check-out date.
  - **ID: price-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter hotels by price range (Budget, Mid-range, Luxury).
  - **ID: hotels-list** - Type: Div - List of available hotels with name, rating, price, and amenities.

### 6. Transportation Page
- **Page Title**: Book Flights
- **Overview**: A page for searching and booking flights with departure and arrival options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: transportation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the transportation page.
  - **ID: departure-city** - Type: Input - Field to enter departure city.
  - **ID: arrival-city** - Type: Input - Field to enter arrival city.
  - **ID: departure-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select departure date.
  - **ID: flight-class-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by flight class (Economy, Business, First Class).
  - **ID: available-flights** - Type: Div - List of available flights with airlines, times, and prices.

### 7. Travel Packages Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Packages
- **Overview**: A page displaying pre-designed travel packages with complete trip information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: packages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the packages page.
  - **ID: packages-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying travel package cards with destination, duration, and price.
  - **ID: duration-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter packages by duration (3-5 days, 7-10 days, 14+ days).
  - **ID: view-package-details-button-{pkg_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view package details (each package has this).
  - **ID: book-package-button-{pkg_id}** - Type: Button - Button to book selected package (each package has this).

### 8. Trip Management Page
- **Page Title**: My Trips
- **Overview**: A page displaying all created trips with options to view, edit, or delete them.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: trips-page** - Type: Div - Container for the trips page.
  - **ID: trips-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all trips with destination, dates, and status.
  - **ID: view-trip-details-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view trip details (each trip has this).
  - **ID: edit-trip-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to edit trip (each trip has this).
  - **ID: delete-trip-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete trip (each trip has this).

### 9. Booking Confirmation Page
- **Page Title**: Booking Confirmation
- **Overview**: A page displaying booking confirmation details with reservation information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: confirmation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the confirmation page.
  - **ID: confirmation-number** - Type: Div - Display confirmation/booking number.
  - **ID: booking-details** - Type: Div - Display detailed booking information (dates, amounts, locations).
  - **ID: download-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to download trip itinerary as PDF.
  - **ID: share-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to share trip details.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Travel Recommendations Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Recommendations
- **Overview**: A page displaying personalized travel recommendations and trending destinations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: recommendations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the recommendations page.
  - **ID: trending-destinations** - Type: Div - Display trending destinations ranked by popularity.
  - **ID: recommendation-season-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by travel season (Spring, Summer, Fall, Winter).
  - **ID: budget-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by budget range (Low, Medium, High).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'TravelPlanner' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Destinations Data
- **File Name**: `destinations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  dest_id|name|country|region|description|attractions|climate
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Paris|France|Europe|City of lights and romance with world-class museums|Eiffel Tower, Louvre Museum, Notre-Dame|Temperate
  2|Tokyo|Japan|Asia|Modern metropolis blending tradition and innovation|Senso-ji Temple, Shibuya Crossing, Meiji Shrine|Temperate
  3|Rio de Janeiro|Brazil|Americas|Vibrant beach city with iconic landmarks|Christ the Redeemer, Copacabana Beach, Sugarloaf Mountain|Tropical
  ```

### 2. Itineraries Data
- **File Name**: `itineraries.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  itinerary_id|itinerary_name|destination|start_date|end_date|activities|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Paris Spring Break|Paris|2025-03-20|2025-03-27|Museum tours, River cruise, Cafe hopping|Planned
  2|Tokyo Adventure|Tokyo|2025-05-01|2025-05-14|Temple visits, Anime district tour, Cooking class|In Progress
  3|Rio Beach Trip|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-15|2025-07-22|Beach days, Hiking, Night clubs|Planned
  ```

### 3. Hotels Data
- **File Name**: `hotels.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  hotel_id|name|city|rating|price_per_night|amenities|category
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Ritz Paris|Paris|5.0|450.00|WiFi, Spa, Restaurant, Pool|Luxury
  2|Hotel Shibuya|Tokyo|4.5|120.00|WiFi, Cafe, Business Center|Mid-range
  3|Copacabana Beach Hotel|Rio de Janeiro|4.0|95.00|Beach access, Restaurant, WiFi|Mid-range
  ```

### 4. Flights Data
- **File Name**: `flights.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  flight_id|airline|departure_city|arrival_city|departure_time|arrival_time|price|class_type|duration
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Air France|New York|Paris|10:00|22:30|850.00|Economy|7 hours 30 minutes
  2|JAL|Los Angeles|Tokyo|14:30|15:20 next day|920.00|Business|11 hours 50 minutes
  3|Latam|Miami|Rio de Janeiro|18:00|23:45|380.00|Economy|5 hours 45 minutes
  ```

### 5. Travel Packages Data
- **File Name**: `packages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  package_id|package_name|destination|duration_days|price|included_items|difficulty_level
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Paris Classic Tour|Paris|5|1500.00|Hotel, Flights, Guided tours, Meals|Easy
  2|Tokyo Experience|Tokyo|10|2200.00|Hotel, Flights, Activities, Cultural events|Moderate
  3|Rio Adventure|Rio de Janeiro|7|1800.00|Hotel, Flights, Beach activities, Mountain hiking|Moderate
  ```

### 6. Trips Data
- **File Name**: `trips.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  trip_id|trip_name|destination|start_date|end_date|total_budget|status|created_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Summer Vacation 2025|Paris|2025-06-01|2025-06-15|3000.00|Booked|2025-01-10
  2|Winter Holiday|Tokyo|2025-12-15|2025-12-30|4500.00|Planned|2025-01-11
  3|Beach Getaway|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-01|2025-07-08|2000.00|Pending|2025-01-12
  ```

### 7. Bookings Data
- **File Name**: `bookings.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  booking_id|trip_id|booking_type|booking_date|amount|confirmation_number|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Hotel|2025-01-10|750.00|CONF001|Confirmed
  2|2|Flight|2025-01-11|1840.00|CONF002|Confirmed
  3|3|Package|2025-01-12|1800.00|CONF003|Pending
  ```

# Requirements Document for 'TravelPlanner' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'TravelPlanner' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse destinations, plan itineraries, search accommodations, book flights, view travel packages, and manage trip details. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'TravelPlanner' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'TravelPlanner' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Planner Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured destinations, upcoming trips, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-destinations** - Type: Div - Display of featured travel destinations.
  - **ID: upcoming-trips** - Type: Div - Display of upcoming planned trips.
  - **ID: browse-destinations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to destinations page.
  - **ID: plan-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to itinerary planning page.

### 2. Destinations Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Destinations
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available travel destinations with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: destinations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the destinations page.
  - **ID: search-destination** - Type: Input - Field to search destinations by name or country.
  - **ID: region-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by region (Asia, Europe, Americas, Africa, Oceania).
  - **ID: destinations-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying destination cards with image, name, and country.
  - **ID: view-destination-button-{dest_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view destination details (each destination card has this).

### 3. Destination Details Page
- **Page Title**: Destination Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific destination.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: destination-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the destination details page.
  - **ID: destination-name** - Type: H1 - Display destination name.
  - **ID: destination-country** - Type: Div - Display destination country.
  - **ID: destination-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description of the destination.
  - **ID: add-to-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to add destination to trip.
  - **ID: destination-attractions** - Type: Div - Section displaying main attractions and activities.

### 4. Itinerary Planning Page
- **Page Title**: Plan Your Itinerary
- **Overview**: A page for users to create and manage travel itineraries with activities and schedules.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: itinerary-page** - Type: Div - Container for the itinerary page.
  - **ID: itinerary-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to enter itinerary name.
  - **ID: start-date-input** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select trip start date.
  - **ID: end-date-input** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select trip end date.
  - **ID: add-activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to add activity to itinerary.
  - **ID: itinerary-list** - Type: Div - Display list of created itineraries with edit/delete options.

### 5. Accommodations Page
- **Page Title**: Search Accommodations
- **Overview**: A page for searching and browsing hotel options with filters and pricing.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: accommodations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the accommodations page.
  - **ID: destination-input** - Type: Input - Field to enter destination city for hotels.
  - **ID: check-in-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select check-in date.
  - **ID: check-out-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select check-out date.
  - **ID: price-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter hotels by price range (Budget, Mid-range, Luxury).
  - **ID: hotels-list** - Type: Div - List of available hotels with name, rating, price, and amenities.

### 6. Transportation Page
- **Page Title**: Book Flights
- **Overview**: A page for searching and booking flights with departure and arrival options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: transportation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the transportation page.
  - **ID: departure-city** - Type: Input - Field to enter departure city.
  - **ID: arrival-city** - Type: Input - Field to enter arrival city.
  - **ID: departure-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select departure date.
  - **ID: flight-class-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by flight class (Economy, Business, First Class).
  - **ID: available-flights** - Type: Div - List of available flights with airlines, times, and prices.

### 7. Travel Packages Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Packages
- **Overview**: A page displaying pre-designed travel packages with complete trip information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: packages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the packages page.
  - **ID: packages-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying travel package cards with destination, duration, and price.
  - **ID: duration-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter packages by duration (3-5 days, 7-10 days, 14+ days).
  - **ID: view-package-details-button-{pkg_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view package details (each package has this).
  - **ID: book-package-button-{pkg_id}** - Type: Button - Button to book selected package (each package has this).

### 8. Trip Management Page
- **Page Title**: My Trips
- **Overview**: A page displaying all created trips with options to view, edit, or delete them.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: trips-page** - Type: Div - Container for the trips page.
  - **ID: trips-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all trips with destination, dates, and status.
  - **ID: view-trip-details-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view trip details (each trip has this).
  - **ID: edit-trip-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to edit trip (each trip has this).
  - **ID: delete-trip-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete trip (each trip has this).

### 9. Booking Confirmation Page
- **Page Title**: Booking Confirmation
- **Overview**: A page displaying booking confirmation details with reservation information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: confirmation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the confirmation page.
  - **ID: confirmation-number** - Type: Div - Display confirmation/booking number.
  - **ID: booking-details** - Type: Div - Display detailed booking information (dates, amounts, locations).
  - **ID: download-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to download trip itinerary as PDF.
  - **ID: share-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to share trip details.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Travel Recommendations Page
- **Page Title**: Travel Recommendations
- **Overview**: A page displaying personalized travel recommendations and trending destinations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: recommendations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the recommendations page.
  - **ID: trending-destinations** - Type: Div - Display trending destinations ranked by popularity.
  - **ID: recommendation-season-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by travel season (Spring, Summer, Fall, Winter).
  - **ID: budget-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by budget range (Low, Medium, High).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

Div `destination-details-page`: Container\n  - H1 `destination-name`: Destination name\n  - Div `destination-country`: Destination country\n  - Div `destination-description`: Detailed description\n  - Div `destination-attractions`: Attractions list\n  - Button `add-to-trip-button`: Button to add destination to itinerary\n- Context Variables:\n  - destination: Dictionary with keys {dest_id: int, name: str, country: str, region: str, description: str}\n  - attractions: List of strings\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `add-to-trip-button`: url_for('itinerary_view')\n\n### 2.4 templates/itinerary.html\n- Page Title: Plan Your Itinerary\n- Elements:\n  - Div `itinerary-page`: Container\n  - Input `itinerary-name-input`: Text input\n  - Input `start-date-input`: Date input\n  - Input `end-date-input`: Date input\n  - Button `add-activity-button`: Adds activities\n  - Div `itinerary-list`: Shows list of itineraries with edit/delete options\n- Context Variables:\n  - itineraries: List of dictionaries {itinerary_id: int, itinerary_name: str, destination: str, start_date: str, end_date: str, activities: str, status: str}\n  - form_errors: Dictionary of validation errors\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Edit/Delete buttons: link to corresponding routes handled with trip IDs\n\n### 2.5 templates/accommodations.html\n- Page Title: Search Accommodations\n- Elements:\n  - Div `accommodations-page`: Container\n  - Input `destination-input`: Text input for city\n  - Input `check-in-date`: Date input\n  - Input `check-out-date`: Date input\n  - Dropdown `price-filter`: Hotel price filter\n  - Div `hotels-list`: List of hotel details\n- Context Variables:\n  - hotels: List of dictionaries {hotel_id: int, name: str, city: str, rating: float, price_per_night: float, amenities: str, category: str}\n  - filters: Dictionary with current filter values\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Filtering triggers page reload with query params\n\n### 2.6 templates/transportation.html\n- Page Title: Book Flights\n- Elements:\n  - Div `transportation-page`: Container\n  - Input `departure-city`: Text input\n  - Input `arrival-city`: Text input\n  - Input `departure-date`: Date input\n  - Dropdown `flight-class-filter`: Flight class selector\n  - Div `available-flights`: List showing flights\n- Context Variables:\n  - flights: List of dictionaries {flight_id: int, airline: str, departure_city: str, arrival_city: str, departure_time: str, arrival_time: str, price: float, class_type: str, duration: str}\n  - filters: Dictionary for current filters\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - Filtering triggers reload with query params\n\n### 2.7 templates/packages.html\n- Page Title: Travel Packages\n- Elements:\n  - Div `packages-page`: Container\n  - Div `packages-grid`: Grid layout of packages\n  - Dropdown `duration-filter`: Filter packages by duration\n  - Buttons with ID patterns `view-package-details-button-{{ pkg.package_id }}` and `book-package-button-{{ pkg.package_id }}`\n- Context Variables:\n  - packages: List of dictionaries {package_id: int, package_name: str, destination: str, duration_days: int, price: float, included_items: str, difficulty_level: str}\n  - duration_filter: Current duration filter string\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - `view-package-details-button-{{ pkg.package_id }}`: url_for('package_detail_view', pkg_id=pkg.package_id)\n  - `book-package-button-{{ pkg.package_id }}`: url_for('book_package', pkg_id=pkg.package_id)\n\n### 2.8 templates/trips.html\n- Page Title: My Trips\n- Elements:\n  - Div `trips-page`: Container\n  - Table `trips-table`: Tabular listing of trips\n  - Buttons with ID patterns `view-trip-details-button-{{ trip.trip_id }}`, `edit-trip-button-{{ trip.trip_id }}`, `delete-trip-button-{{ trip.trip_id }}`\n- Context Variables:\n  - trips: List of dictionaries {trip_id: int, trip_name: str, destination: str, start_date: str, end_date: str, total_budget: float, status: str, created_date: str}\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - View/Edit/Delete buttons: url_for with respective trip_id\n\n### 2.9 templates/booking_confirmation.html\n- Page Title: Booking Confirmation\n- Elements:\n  - Div `confirmation-page`: Container\n  - Div `confirmation-number`: Booking number display\n  - Div `booking-details`: Booking info details\n  - Button `download-itinerary-button`: Initiates itinerary download (PDF)\n  - Button `share-trip-button`: Share trip details\n  - Button `back-to-dashboard`: Navigate to dashboard\n- Context Variables:\n  - booking: Dictionary of booking data\n  - trip: Dictionary of related trip data\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - back-to-dashboard: url_for('dashboard_view')\n\n### 2.10 templates/recommendations.html\n- Page Title: Travel Recommendations\n- Elements:\n  - Div `recommendations-page`: Container\n  - Div `trending-destinations`: Trending destinations display\n  - Dropdown `recommendation-season-filter`: Filter by season\n  - Dropdown `budget-filter`: Budget filter\n  - Button `back-to-dashboard`: Navigate to Dashboard\n- Context Variables:\n  - recommendations: List of dicts with recommended trips/destinations\n  - filters: Dictionary of current filters\n- Navigation Mappings:\n  - back-to-dashboard: url_for('dashboard_view')\n\n---\n\n## 3. Data File Schemas\n\n### 3.1 data/destinations.txt\n- Field Order and Names:\n  dest_id|name|country|region|description|attractions|climate\n- Description: Information about travel destinations\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Paris|France|Europe|City of lights and romance with world-class museums|Eiffel Tower, Louvre Museum, Notre-Dame|Temperate\n  2|Tokyo|Japan|Asia|Modern metropolis blending tradition and innovation|Senso-ji Temple, Shibuya Crossing, Meiji Shrine|Temperate\n  3|Rio de Janeiro|Brazil|Americas|Vibrant beach city with iconic landmarks|Christ the Redeemer, Copacabana Beach, Sugarloaf Mountain|Tropical\n  ```\n- No header row\n\n### 3.2 data/itineraries.txt\n- Field Order and Names:\n  itinerary_id|itinerary_name|destination|start_date|end_date|activities|status\n- Description: User created travel itineraries\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Paris Spring Break|Paris|2025-03-20|2025-03-27|Museum tours, River cruise, Cafe hopping|Planned\n  2|Tokyo Adventure|Tokyo|2025-05-01|2025-05-14|Temple visits, Anime district tour, Cooking class|In Progress\n  3|Rio Beach Trip|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-15|2025-07-22|Beach days, Hiking, Night clubs|Planned\n  ```\n- No header row\n\n### 3.3 data/hotels.txt\n- Field Order and Names:\n  hotel_id|name|city|rating|price_per_night|amenities|category\n- Description: Available hotels data\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Ritz Paris|Paris|5.0|450.00|WiFi, Spa, Restaurant, Pool|Luxury\n  2|Hotel Shibuya|Tokyo|4.5|120.00|WiFi, Cafe, Business Center|Mid-range\n  3|Copacabana Beach Hotel|Rio de Janeiro|4.0|95.00|Beach access, Restaurant, WiFi|Mid-range\n  ```\n- No header row\n\n### 3.4 data/flights.txt\n- Field Order and Names:\n  flight_id|airline|departure_city|arrival_city|departure_time|arrival_time|price|class_type|duration\n- Description: Flights data for bookings\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Air France|New York|Paris|10:00|22:30|850.00|Economy|7 hours 30 minutes\n  2|JAL|Los Angeles|Tokyo|14:30|15:20 next day|920.00|Business|11 hours 50 minutes\n  3|Latam|Miami|Rio de Janeiro|18:00|23:45|380.00|Economy|5 hours 45 minutes\n  ```\n- No header row\n\n### 3.5 data/packages.txt\n- Field Order and Names:\n  package_id|package_name|destination|duration_days|price|included_items|difficulty_level\n- Description: Pre-designed travel packages\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Paris Classic Tour|Paris|5|1500.00|Hotel, Flights, Guided tours, Meals|Easy\n  2|Tokyo Experience|Tokyo|10|2200.00|Hotel, Flights, Activities, Cultural events|Moderate\n  3|Rio Adventure|Rio de Janeiro|7|1800.00|Hotel, Flights, Beach activities, Mountain hiking|Moderate\n  ```\n- No header row\n\n### 3.6 data/trips.txt\n- Field Order and Names:\n  trip_id|trip_name|destination|start_date|end_date|total_budget|status|created_date\n- Description: User trips data\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|Summer Vacation 2025|Paris|2025-06-01|2025-06-15|3000.00|Booked|2025-01-10\n  2|Winter Holiday|Tokyo|2025-12-15|2025-12-30|4500.00|Planned|2025-01-11\n  3|Beach Getaway|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-01|2025-07-08|2000.00|Pending|2025-01-12\n  ```\n- No header row\n\n### 3.7 data/bookings.txt\n- Field Order and Names:\n  booking_id|trip_id|booking_type|booking_date|amount|confirmation_number|status\n- Description: Booking confirmations data\n- Example:\n  ```\n  1|1|Hotel|2025-01-10|750.00|CONF001|Confirmed\n  2|2|Flight|2025-01-11|1840.00|CONF002|Confirmed\n  3|3|Package|2025-01-12|1800.00|CONF003|Pending\n  ```\n- No header row\n\n---\n\nThis detailed design specification fully supports independent backend and frontend development of the TravelPlanner web application. It provides complete Flask route definitions, template element specifications, context variables, and data file schemas.\n"})

  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'TravelPlanner' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'TravelPlanner' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse destinations, plan itineraries, search accommodations, book flights, view travel packages, and manage trip details. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'TravelPlanner' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'TravelPlanner' web application will consist of the following ten pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Travel Planner Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured destinations, upcoming trips, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-destinations** - Type: Div - Display of featured travel destinations.   - **ID: upcoming-trips** - Type: Div - Display of upcoming planned trips.   - **ID: browse-destinations-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to destinations page.   - **ID: plan-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to itinerary planning page.  ### 2. Destinations Page - **Page Title**: Travel Destinations - **Overview**: A page displaying all available travel destinations with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: destinations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the destinations page.   - **ID: search-destination** - Type: Input - Field to search destinations by name or country.   - **ID: region-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by region (Asia, Europe, Americas, Africa, Oceania).   - **ID: destinations-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying destination cards with image, name, and country.   - **ID: view-destination-button-{dest_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view destination details (each destination card has this).  ### 3. Destination Details Page - **Page Title**: Destination Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific destination. - **Elements**:   - **ID: destination-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the destination details page.   - **ID: destination-name** - Type: H1 - Display destination name.   - **ID: destination-country** - Type: Div - Display destination country.   - **ID: destination-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description of the destination.   - **ID: add-to-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to add destination to trip.   - **ID: destination-attractions** - Type: Div - Section displaying main attractions and activities.  ### 4. Itinerary Planning Page - **Page Title**: Plan Your Itinerary - **Overview**: A page for users to create and manage travel itineraries with activities and schedules. - **Elements**:   - **ID: itinerary-page** - Type: Div - Container for the itinerary page.   - **ID: itinerary-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to enter itinerary name.   - **ID: start-date-input** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select trip start date.   - **ID: end-date-input** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select trip end date.   - **ID: add-activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to add activity to itinerary.   - **ID: itinerary-list** - Type: Div - Display list of created itineraries with edit/delete options.  ### 5. Accommodations Page - **Page Title**: Search Accommodations - **Overview**: A page for searching and browsing hotel options with filters and pricing. - **Elements**:   - **ID: accommodations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the accommodations page.   - **ID: destination-input** - Type: Input - Field to enter destination city for hotels.   - **ID: check-in-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select check-in date.   - **ID: check-out-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select check-out date.   - **ID: price-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter hotels by price range (Budget, Mid-range, Luxury).   - **ID: hotels-list** - Type: Div - List of available hotels with name, rating, price, and amenities.  ### 6. Transportation Page - **Page Title**: Book Flights - **Overview**: A page for searching and booking flights with departure and arrival options. - **Elements**:   - **ID: transportation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the transportation page.   - **ID: departure-city** - Type: Input - Field to enter departure city.   - **ID: arrival-city** - Type: Input - Field to enter arrival city.   - **ID: departure-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to select departure date.   - **ID: flight-class-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by flight class (Economy, Business, First Class).   - **ID: available-flights** - Type: Div - List of available flights with airlines, times, and prices.  ### 7. Travel Packages Page - **Page Title**: Travel Packages - **Overview**: A page displaying pre-designed travel packages with complete trip information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: packages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the packages page.   - **ID: packages-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying travel package cards with destination, duration, and price.   - **ID: duration-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter packages by duration (3-5 days, 7-10 days, 14+ days).   - **ID: view-package-details-button-{pkg_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view package details (each package has this).   - **ID: book-package-button-{pkg_id}** - Type: Button - Button to book selected package (each package has this).  ### 8. Trip Management Page - **Page Title**: My Trips - **Overview**: A page displaying all created trips with options to view, edit, or delete them. - **Elements**:   - **ID: trips-page** - Type: Div - Container for the trips page.   - **ID: trips-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all trips with destination, dates, and status.   - **ID: view-trip-details-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view trip details (each trip has this).   - **ID: edit-trip-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to edit trip (each trip has this).   - **ID: delete-trip-button-{trip_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete trip (each trip has this).  ### 9. Booking Confirmation Page - **Page Title**: Booking Confirmation - **Overview**: A page displaying booking confirmation details with reservation information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: confirmation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the confirmation page.   - **ID: confirmation-number** - Type: Div - Display confirmation/booking number.   - **ID: booking-details** - Type: Div - Display detailed booking information (dates, amounts, locations).   - **ID: download-itinerary-button** - Type: Button - Button to download trip itinerary as PDF.   - **ID: share-trip-button** - Type: Button - Button to share trip details.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 10. Travel Recommendations Page - **Page Title**: Travel Recommendations - **Overview**: A page displaying personalized travel recommendations and trending destinations. - **Elements**:   - **ID: recommendations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the recommendations page.   - **ID: trending-destinations** - Type: Div - Display trending destinations ranked by popularity.   - **ID: recommendation-season-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by travel season (Spring, Summer, Fall, Winter).   - **ID: budget-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by budget range (Low, Medium, High).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'TravelPlanner' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Destinations Data - **File Name**: `destinations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   dest_id|name|country|region|description|attractions|climate   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Paris|France|Europe|City of lights and romance with world-class museums|Eiffel Tower, Louvre Museum, Notre-Dame|Temperate   2|Tokyo|Japan|Asia|Modern metropolis blending tradition and innovation|Senso-ji Temple, Shibuya Crossing, Meiji Shrine|Temperate   3|Rio de Janeiro|Brazil|Americas|Vibrant beach city with iconic landmarks|Christ the Redeemer, Copacabana Beach, Sugarloaf Mountain|Tropical   ```  ### 2. Itineraries Data - **File Name**: `itineraries.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   itinerary_id|itinerary_name|destination|start_date|end_date|activities|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Paris Spring Break|Paris|2025-03-20|2025-03-27|Museum tours, River cruise, Cafe hopping|Planned   2|Tokyo Adventure|Tokyo|2025-05-01|2025-05-14|Temple visits, Anime district tour, Cooking class|In Progress   3|Rio Beach Trip|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-15|2025-07-22|Beach days, Hiking, Night clubs|Planned   ```  ### 3. Hotels Data - **File Name**: `hotels.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   hotel_id|name|city|rating|price_per_night|amenities|category   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Ritz Paris|Paris|5.0|450.00|WiFi, Spa, Restaurant, Pool|Luxury   2|Hotel Shibuya|Tokyo|4.5|120.00|WiFi, Cafe, Business Center|Mid-range   3|Copacabana Beach Hotel|Rio de Janeiro|4.0|95.00|Beach access, Restaurant, WiFi|Mid-range   ```  ### 4. Flights Data - **File Name**: `flights.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   flight_id|airline|departure_city|arrival_city|departure_time|arrival_time|price|class_type|duration   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Air France|New York|Paris|10:00|22:30|850.00|Economy|7 hours 30 minutes   2|JAL|Los Angeles|Tokyo|14:30|15:20 next day|920.00|Business|11 hours 50 minutes   3|Latam|Miami|Rio de Janeiro|18:00|23:45|380.00|Economy|5 hours 45 minutes   ```  ### 5. Travel Packages Data - **File Name**: `packages.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   package_id|package_name|destination|duration_days|price|included_items|difficulty_level   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Paris Classic Tour|Paris|5|1500.00|Hotel, Flights, Guided tours, Meals|Easy   2|Tokyo Experience|Tokyo|10|2200.00|Hotel, Flights, Activities, Cultural events|Moderate   3|Rio Adventure|Rio de Janeiro|7|1800.00|Hotel, Flights, Beach activities, Mountain hiking|Moderate   ```  ### 6. Trips Data - **File Name**: `trips.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   trip_id|trip_name|destination|start_date|end_date|total_budget|status|created_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Summer Vacation 2025|Paris|2025-06-01|2025-06-15|3000.00|Booked|2025-01-10   2|Winter Holiday|Tokyo|2025-12-15|2025-12-30|4500.00|Planned|2025-01-11   3|Beach Getaway|Rio de Janeiro|2025-07-01|2025-07-08|2000.00|Pending|2025-01-12   ```  ### 7. Bookings Data - **File Name**: `bookings.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   booking_id|trip_id|booking_type|booking_date|amount|confirmation_number|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Hotel|2025-01-10|750.00|CONF001|Confirmed   2|2|Flight|2025-01-11|1840.00|CONF002|Confirmed   3|3|Package|2025-01-12|1800.00|CONF003|Pending   ```
